# Firefox DOM Event Dispatch Chain

## Your Task

Trace how a DOM event (e.g., click) is dispatched through the Firefox event system in mozilla/gecko-dev. Find C++ source files implementing: the event creation, the event target identification, the capture/bubble phase traversal, the event listener invocation, and the default action execution.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/firefox--871325b8.

The answer has been written to `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Firefox DOM Event Dispatch Chain

The event dispatch chain in Firefox (gecko-dev) flows through these key stages:

### 1. Entry Point — `layout/base/PresShell.cpp`
- `PresShell::HandleEvent()` receives raw GUI events from the widget layer and performs hit-testing to identify the target frame/content node.
- `PresShell::EventHandler::DispatchEvent()` orchestrates the full three-phase dispatch.

### 2. Pre-dispatch — `dom/events/EventStateManager.cpp`
- `EventStateManager::PreHandleEvent()` handles :hover/:active state, mouse boundary event synthesis, and user activity tracking before the DOM sees the event.

### 3. Event Target Chain Construction — `dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp`
- `EventDispatcher::Dispatch()` builds an `nsTArray<EventTargetChainItem>` by walking up from the target, calling `GetEventTargetParent()` on each node.
- **`dom/base/FragmentOrElement.cpp`** — `nsIContent::GetEventTargetParent()` walks the DOM tree, handles Shadow DOM retargeting and anonymous content boundaries.

### 4. Capture/Bubble Traversal — `dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp`
- `EventTargetChainItem::HandleEventTargetChain()` does a two-pass iteration: first downward (capture), then upward (bubble), calling `HandleEvent()` on each chain item.

### 5. Listener Invocation — `dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp`
- `HandleEventInternal()` → `HandleEventWithListenerArray()` → `HandleEventSingleListener()` — finds and invokes all registered JS/native event handlers for the current phase.

### 6. Default Actions — `dom/events/EventStateManager.cpp`
- `EventStateManager::PostHandleEvent()` processes browser-default behaviors (click generation on mouseup, link activation, scrolling for wheel events, drag-d
... (truncated)

It handles browser default behaviors based on event type:\\n- For `eMouseDown`: sets mouse capture, records click targets.\\n- For `eMouseUp`: dispatches synthesized `click` and `dblclick` events.\\n- For `eKeyPress`: processes keyboard shortcuts and character input.\\n- For wheel events: initiates scrolling via `WheelHandlingHelper`.\\n- For `eDrop`: handles drag-and-drop completion.\\n\\nThe `EventTargetChainItem::ActivationBehavior()` method (line 465 of EventDispatcher.cpp) handles the HTML activation behavior (e.g., following links, submitting forms) per the DOM spec's activation behavior model.\\n\\n## Summary Flow\\n\\n```\\nWidget input event\\n  \u2192 PresShell::HandleEvent()          [layout/base/PresShell.cpp]\\n    \u2192 PresShell::EventHandler::DispatchEvent()\\n      \u2192 EventStateManager::PreHandleEvent()   [dom/events/EventStateManager.cpp]\\n      \u2192 PresShell::EventHandler::DispatchEventToDOM()\\n        \u2192 EventDispatcher::Dispatch()         [dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp]\\n          \u2192 EventTargetChainItem::GetEventTargetParent() (builds chain)\\n            \u2192 nsIContent::GetEventTargetParent()  [dom/base/FragmentOrElement.cpp]\\n          \u2192 EventTargetChainItem::HandleEventTargetChain() (capture/bubble)\\n            \u2192 EventTargetChainItem::HandleEvent() (per node)\\n              \u2192 EventListenerManager::HandleEventInternal()  [dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp]\\n                \u2192 HandleEventWithListenerArray()\\n                  \u2192 HandleEventSingleListener()  (invokes JS/native handlers)\\n            \u2192 EventTargetChainItem::PostHandleEvent()\\n            \u2192 EventTargetChainItem::ActivationBehavior()\\n      \u2192 EventStateManager::PostHandleEvent()  (default actions / synthesis)\\n```\"\n}\n",
